name:Wâ€oâ€bâ€uâ€sâ€hâ€iâ€Nâ€Oâ€Nâ€O
info:Guestroom (2 beds)
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Business travelers
info:4 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted December 8, 2023
msg:The hotel is in a very good location. Downstairs is the Xizi International shopping mall, which has many restaurants and is convenient for dining.
The room facilities are relatively new and business-style. It is still very cost-effective for this price range. The bedding is slightly soft, but it is also acceptable.
The room is very clean. Both the floor tiles and the carpet are very satisfactory, but there is also a very big disadvantage, that is, the water pressure of the shower is too low. It feels like a tear shower, which is really not right in such a quasi-five-star hotel.
The breakfast variety is not too much, and it is also quite satisfactory. What I am not satisfied with is that the juice is all machine-made, that is, it is soaked. At least there should be fresh juice.
